\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ syscall/malloc\ can\ set\ non-\/zero\ errno\ in\ case\ of\ failure,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ but\ later\ allocator\ might\ be\ able\ to\ find\ memory\ to\ fulfill\ the\ request.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00029\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ And\ we\ do\ not\ want\ changing\ of\ errno\ by\ successful\ scalable\_malloc\ call.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ To\ support\ this,\ restore\ old\ errno\ in\ (get|free)RawMemory,\ and\ set\ errno}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00031\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ in\ frontend\ just\ before\ returning\ to\ user\ code.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Please\ note:\ every\ syscall/libc\ call\ used\ inside\ scalable\_malloc\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00033\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ sets\ errno\ must\ be\ protected\ this\ way,\ not\ just\ memory\ allocation\ per\ se.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00034\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
